PUBLIC NOTICE
ITI CAPITAL MARKETS LIMITED
Registered Office: Century Centre, 75, T.T.K. Road, Alwarpet, Chennai-600 018.
Notice pursuant to Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, is hereby given for general information, that the Members
of ITI CAPITAL MARKETS LIMITED, at the adjourned Annual General Meeting of the Company held on December 3, 2015
at its Registered Office of the Company, have passed the following special resolution to wind up the above said Company
by Members’ Voluntary Winding up.
Members’ Voluntary winding up of the Company:
“RESOLVED THAT, pursuant to the Declaration of Solvency made by the Board of Directors of the Company in their
meeting held on October 29, 2015 and duly filed with Registrar of Companies, Chennai and section 484(1) (b) of the
Companies Act, 1956 [subject to any statutory modification(s) or re-enactment(s) thereof, for the time being in force] and
other applicable provisions, if any, the Company be wound up voluntarily;
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT all the statutory records of the Company be preserved for a period of five years from the
date of dissolution of the Company and that after the said five years, the records shall be dealt with in the best possible
manner and that the liquidator so appointed be authorized to do all such necessary acts, deeds, and things to deal with the
records, including but not limited to preserving or disposing them, to give full effect to this resolution.”

Chennai,

ITI Capital Markets Limited.

16th December 2015.

JAYARAM SUBRAMANIAM,
Liquidator.
